      ( ( ($A * $B) --> $R) $True))

;;other direction of same rules (as these are bi-directional)
  ; Action: load=metta_defn('&self',['|-',[[A,-->,[R,'/1',B]],True]],[[[A,*,B],-->,R],['Truth_StructuralIntersection',True]])
  (= 
    ("|-" 
      ( ($A --> 
          ($R "/1" $B)) $True)) 
    ( ( ($A * $B) --> $R) 
      (Truth_StructuralIntersection $True)))


  ; Action: load=metta_defn('&self',['|-',[[B,-->,[R,'/2',A]],True]],[[[A,*,B],-->,R],['Truth_StructuralIntersection',True]])
  (= 
    ("|-" 
      ( ($B --> 
          ($R "/2" $A)) $True)) 
    ( ( ($A * $B) --> $R) 
      (Truth_StructuralIntersection $True)))


  ; Action: load=metta_defn('&self',['|-',[[[R,'\\1',B],-->,A],True]],[[R,-->,[A,*,B]],['Truth_StructuralIntersection',True]])
  (= 
    ("|-" 
      ( ( ($R \1 $B) --> $A) $True)) 
    ( ($R --> 
        ($A * $B)) 
      (Truth_StructuralIntersection $True)))

  ; Action: load=metta_defn('&self',['|-',[[[R,'\\2',A],-->,B],True]],[[R,-->,[A,*,B]],['Truth_StructuralIntersection',True]])

;;!Comparative relations
  ; Action: load=metta_defn('&self',['|-',[[[{},R],'|-',>,[['[]',P]]],T1],[[[{},S],'|-',>,[['[]',P]]],T2]],[[[[{},R],*,[{},S]],-->,[>>>,P]],['Truth_FrequencyGreater',T1,T2]])
  (= 
    ("|-" 
      ( ( ({} $R) "|-" > 
          ( ([] $P))) $T1) 
      ( ( ({} $S) "|-" > 
          ( ([] $P))) $T2)) 
    ( ( ( ({} $R) * 
          ({} $S)) --> 
        (>>> $P)) 
      (Truth_FrequencyGreater $T1 $T2)))

  ; Action: load=metta_defn('&self',['|-',[[R,-->,[A,*,B]],T1],[[C,-->,A],T2]],[[R,-->,[C,*,B]],['Truth_Abduction',T1,T2]])
  (= 
    ("|-" 
      ( ($R --> 
          ($A * $B)) $T1) 
      ( ($C --> $A) $T2)) 
    ( ($R --> 
        ($C * $B)) 
      (Truth_Abduction $T1 $T2)))


  ; Action: load=metta_defn('&self',['|-',[[R,-->,[A,*,B]],T1],[[C,<->,A],T2]],[[R,-->,[C,*,B]],['Truth_Analogy',T1,T2]])
  (= 
    ("|-" 
      ( ($R --> 
          ($A * $B)) $T1) 
      ( ($C <-> $A) $T2)) 
    ( ($R --> 
        ($C * $B)) 
      (Truth_Analogy $T1 $T2)))


  ; Action: load=metta_defn('&self',['|-',[[R,-->,[A,*,B]],T1],[[B,-->,C],T2]],[[R,-->,[A,*,C]],['Truth_Deduction',T1,T2]])
  (= 
    ("|-" 
      ( ($R --> 
          ($A * $B)) $T1) 
      ( ($B --> $C) $T2)) 
    ( ($R --> 
        ($A * $C)) 
      (Truth_Deduction $T1 $T2)))


  ; Action: load=metta_defn('&self',['|-',[[R,-->,[A,*,B]],T1],[[C,-->,B],T2]],[[R,-->,[A,*,C]],['Truth_Abduction',T1,T2]])
  (= 
    ("|-" 
      ( ($R --> 
          ($A * $B)) $T1) 
      ( ($C --> $B) $T2)) 
    ( ($R --> 
        ($A * $C)) 
      (Truth_Abduction $T1 $T2)))


  ; Action: load=metta_defn('&self',['|-',[[R,-->,[A,*,B]],T1],[[C,<->,B],T2]],[[R,-->,[A,*,C]],['Truth_Analogy',T1,T2]])
  (= 
    ("|-" 
      ( ($R --> 
          ($A * $B)) $T1) 
      ( ($C <-> $B) $T2)) 
    ( ($R --> 
        ($A * $C)) 
      (Truth_Analogy $T1 $T2)))


  ; Action: load=metta_defn('&self',['|-',[[[A,*,B],-->,R],T1],[[[C,*,B],-->,R],T2]],[[A,<->,C],['Truth_Comparison',T1,T2]])
  (= 
    ("|-" 
      ( ( ($A * $B) --> $R) $T1) 
      ( ( ($C * $B) --> $R) $T2)) 
    ( ($A <-> $C) 
      (Truth_Comparison $T1 $T2)))

;;NAL-5
;;!Negation conjunction and disjunction decomposition:
  ; Action: load=metta_defn('&self',['|-',[[!,A],True]],[A,['Truth_Negation',True]])
  (= 
    ("|-" 
      ( (! $A) $True)) 
    ($A 
      (Truth_Negation $True)))


  ; Action: load=metta_defn('&self',['|-',[[A,&&,B],True]],[A,['Truth_StructuralDeduction',True]])
  (= 
    ("|-" 
      ( ($A && $B) $True)) 
    ($A 
      (Truth_StructuralDeduction $True)))


  ; Action: load=metta_defn('&self',['|-',[[A,&&,B],True]],[B,['Truth_StructuralDeduction',True]])
  (= 
    ("|-" 
      ( ($A && $B) $True)) 
    ($B 
      (Truth_StructuralDeduction $True)))


  ; Action: load=metta_defn('&self',['|-',[[A,&&,B],True]],[[B,&&,A],['Truth_StructuralIntersection',True]])
  (= 
    ("|-" 
      ( ($A && $B) $True)) 
    ( ($B && $A) 
      (Truth_StructuralIntersection $True)))


  ; Action: load=metta_defn('&self',['|-',[S,T1],[[S,&&,A],T2]],[A,['Truth_DecomposePNN',T1,T2]])
  (= 
    ("|-" 
      ($S $T1) 
      ( ($S && $A) $T2)) 
    ($A 
      (Truth_DecomposePNN $T1 $T2)))


  ; Action: load=metta_defn('&self',['|-',[S,T1],[[S,'||',A],T2]],[A,['Truth_DecomposeNPP',T1,T2]])
  (= 
    ("|-" 
      ($S $T1) 
      ( ($S "||" $A) $T2)) 
    ($A 
      (Truth_DecomposeNPP $T1 $T2)))


  ; Action: load=metta_defn('&self',['|-',[S,T1],[[[!,S],&&,A],T2]],[A,['Truth_DecomposeNNN',T1,T2]])
  (= 
    ("|-" 
      ($S $T1) 
      ( ( (! $S) && $A) $T2)) 
    ($A 
      (Truth_DecomposeNNN $T1 $T2)))


  ; Action: load=metta_defn('&self',['|-',[S,T1],[[[!,S],'||',A],T2]],[A,['Truth_DecomposePPP',T1,T2]])
  (= 
    ("|-" 
      ($S $T1) 
      ( ( (! $S) "||" $A) $T2)) 
    ($A 
      (Truth_DecomposePPP $T1 $T2)))


;;!Syllogistic rules for Implication:
  ; Action: load=metta_defn('&self',['|-',[[A,==>,B],T1],[[B,==>,C],T2]],[[A,==>,C],['Truth_Deduction',T1,T2]])
  (= 
    ("|-" 
      ( ($A ==> $B) $T1) 
      ( ($B ==> $C) $T2)) 
    ( ($A ==> $C) 
      (Truth_Deduction $T1 $T2)))


  ; Action: load=metta_defn('&self',['|-',[[A,==>,B],T1],[[A,==>,C],T2]],[[C,==>,B],['Truth_Induction',T1,T2]])
  (= 
    ("|-" 
      ( ($A ==> $B) $T1) 
      ( ($A ==> $C) $T2)) 
    ( ($C ==> $B) 
      (Truth_Induction $T1 $T2)))


  ; Action: load=metta_defn('&self',['|-',[[A,==>,C],T1],[[B,==>,C],T2]],[[B,==>,A],['Truth_Abduction',T1,T2]])
  (= 
    ("|-" 
      ( ($A ==> $C) $T1) 
      ( ($B ==> $C) $T2)) 
    ( ($B ==> $A) 
      (Truth_Abduction $T1 $T2)))


  ; Action: load=metta_defn('&self',['|-',[[A,==>,B],T1],[[B,==>,C],T2]],[[C,==>,A],['Truth_Exemplification',T1,T2]])
  (= 
    ("|-" 
      ( ($A ==> $B) $T1) 
      ( ($B ==> $C) $T2)) 
    ( ($C ==> $A) 
      (Truth_Exemplification $T1 $T2)))


;;!Conditional composition for conjunction and disjunction:
  ; Action: load=metta_defn('&self',['|-',[[A,==>,C],T1],[[B,==>,C],T2]],[[[A,&&,B],==>,C],['Truth_Union',T1,T2]])
  (= 
    ("|-" 
      ( ($A ==> $C) $T1) 
      ( ($B ==> $C) $T2)) 
    ( ( ($A && $B) ==> $C) 
      (Truth_Union $T1 $T2)))


  ; Action: load=metta_defn('&self',['|-',[[A,==>,C],T1],[[B,==>,C],T2]],[[[A,'||',B],==>,C],['Truth_Intersection',T1,T2]])
  (= 
    ("|-" 
      ( ($A ==> $C) $T1) 
      ( ($B ==> $C) $T2)) 
    ( ( ($A "||" $B) ==> $C) 
      (Truth_Intersection $T1 $T2)))


  ; Action: load=metta_defn('&self',['|-',[[C,==>,A],T1],[[C,==>,B],T2]],[[C,==>,[A,&&,B]],['Truth_Intersection',T1,T2]])
  (= 
    ("|-" 
      ( ($C ==> $A) $T1) 
      ( ($C ==> $B) $T2)) 
    ( ($C ==> 
        ($A && $B)) 
      (Truth_Intersection $T1 $T2)))


  ; Action: load=metta_defn('&self',['|-',[[C,==>,A],T1],[[C,==>,B],T2]],[[C,==>,[A,'||',B]],['Truth_Union',T1,T2]])
  (= 
    ("|-" 
      ( ($C ==> $A) $T1) 
      ( ($C ==> $B) $T2)) 
    ( ($C ==> 
        ($A "||" $B)) 
      (Truth_Union $T1 $T2)))


;;!Multi-conditional inference:
  ; Action: load=metta_defn('&self',['|-',[[[S,&&,P],==>,M],T1],[[S,==>,M],T2]],[P,['Truth_Abduction',T1,T2]])
  (= 
    ("|-" 
      ( ( ($S && $P) ==> $M) $T1) 
      ( ($S ==> $M) $T2)) 
    ($P 
      (Truth_Abduction $T1 $T2)))


  ; Action: load=metta_defn('&self',['|-',[[[C,&&,M],==>,P],T1],[[S,==>,M],T2]],[[[C,&&,S],==>,P],['Truth_Deduction',T1,T2]])
  (= 
    ("|-" 
      ( ( ($C && $M) ==> $P) $T1) 
      ( ($S ==> $M) $T2)) 
    ( ( ($C && $S) ==> $P) 
      (Truth_Deduction $T1 $T2)))


  ; Action: load=metta_defn('&self',['|-',[[[C,&&,P],==>,M],T1],[[[C,&&,S],==>,M],T2]],[[S,==>,P],['Truth_Abduction',T1,T2]])
  (= 
    ("|-" 
      ( ( ($C && $P) ==> $M) $T1) 
      ( ( ($C && $S) ==> $M) $T2)) 
    ( ($S ==> $P) 
      (Truth_Abduction $T1 $T2)))


  ; Action: load=metta_defn('&self',['|-',[[[C,&&,M],==>,P],T1],[[M,==>,S],T2]],[[[C,&&,S],==>,P],['Truth_Induction',T1,T2]])
  (= 
    ("|-" 
      ( ( ($C && $M) ==> $P) $T1) 
      ( ($M ==> $S) $T2)) 
    ( ( ($C && $S) ==> $P) 
      (Truth_Induction $T1 $T2)))


;;!Rules for equivalence:
  ; Action: load=metta_defn('&self',['|-',[[S,<=>,P],True]],[[P,<=>,S],['Truth_StructuralIntersection',True]])
  (= 
    ("|-" 
      ( ($S <=> $P) $True)) 
    ( ($P <=> $S) 
      (Truth_StructuralIntersection $True)))


  ; Action: load=metta_defn('&self',['|-',[[S,==>,P],T1],[[P,==>,S],T2]],[[S,<=>,P],['Truth_Intersection',T1,T2]])
  (= 
    ("|-" 
      ( ($S ==> $P) $T1) 
      ( ($P ==> $S) $T2)) 
    ( ($S <=> $P) 
      (Truth_Intersection $T1 $T2)))


  ; Action: load=metta_defn('&self',['|-',[[P,==>,M],T1],[[S,==>,M],T2]],[[S,<=>,P],['Truth_Comparison',T1,T2]])
  (= 
    ("|-" 
      ( ($P ==> $M) $T1) 
      ( ($S ==> $M) $T2)) 
    ( ($S <=> $P) 
      (Truth_Comparison $T1 $T2)))


  ; Action: load=metta_defn('&self',['|-',[[M,==>,P],T1],[[M,==>,S],T2]],[[S,<=>,P],['Truth_Comparison',T1,T2]])
  (= 
    ("|-" 
      ( ($M ==> $P) $T1) 
      ( ($M ==> $S) $T2)) 
    ( ($S <=> $P) 
      (Truth_Comparison $T1 $T2)))


!(assertEqualToResult (sample (SecondOrderHybridDist)) ((thunk (f (sample (Bernoulli)))) (thunk (HybridPerm (sample (HybridDist))))))

!(assertEqualToResult (sample (SecondOrderHybridDist)) ((thunk (f (sample (Bernoulli)))) (thunk (HybridPerm (sample (HybridDist))))))

  ; Action: load=metta_defn('&self',['|-',[[M,==>,P],T1],[[S,<=>,M],T2]],[[S,==>,P],['Truth_Analogy',T1,T2]])
  (= 
    ("|-" 
      ( ($M ==> $P) $T1) 
      ( ($S <=> $M) $T2)) 
    ( ($S ==> $P) 
      (Truth_Analogy $T1 $T2)))


  ; Action: load=metta_defn('&self',['|-',[[P,==>,M],T1],[[S,<=>,M],T2]],[[P,==>,S],['Truth_Analogy',T1,T2]])
  (= 
    ("|-" 
      ( ($P ==> $M) $T1) 
      ( ($S <=> $M) $T2)) 
    ( ($P ==> $S) 
      (Truth_Analogy $T1 $T2)))


  ; Action: load=metta_defn('&self',['|-',[[M,<=>,P],T1],[[S,<=>,M],T2]],[[S,<=>,P],['Truth_Resemblance',T1,T2]])
  (= 
    ("|-" 
      ( ($M <=> $P) $T1) 
      ( ($S <=> $M) $T2)) 
    ( ($S <=> $P) 
      (Truth_Resemblance $T1 $T2)))


;;!Higher-order decomposition
  ; Action: load=metta_defn('&self',['|-',[A,T1],[[A,==>,B],T2]],[B,['Truth_Deduction',T1,T2]])
  (= 
    ("|-" 
      ($A $T1) 
      ( ($A ==> $B) $T2)) 
    ($B 
      (Truth_Deduction $T1 $T2)))


  ; Action: load=metta_defn('&self',['|-',[A,T1],[[[A,&&,B],==>,C],T2]],[[B,==>,C],['Truth_Deduction',T1,T2]])
  (= 
    ("|-" 
      ($A $T1) 
      ( ( ($A && $B) ==> $C) $T2)) 
    ( ($B ==> $C) 
      (Truth_Deduction $T1 $T2)))


  ; Action: load=metta_defn('&self',['|-',[B,T1],[[A,==>,B],T2]],[A,['Truth_Abduction',T1,T2]])
  (= 
    ("|-" 
      ($B $T1) 
      ( ($A ==> $B) $T2)) 
    ($A 
      (Truth_Abduction $T1 $T2)))


  ; Action: load=metta_defn('&self',['|-',[A,T1],[[A,<=>,B],T2]],[B,['Truth_Analogy',T1,T2]])
  (= 
    ("|-" 
      ($A $T1) 
      ( ($A <=> $B) $T2)) 
    ($B 
      (Truth_Analogy $T1 $T2)))


;;NAL term reductions
;;!Extensional intersection, union, conjunction reductions:
  ; Action: load=metta_defn('&self',[A,&,A],A)
  (= 
    ($A & $A) $A)


  ; Action: load=metta_defn('&self',[A,'|',A],A)
  (= 
    ($A "|" $A) $A)


  ; Action: load=metta_defn('&self',[A,&&,A],A)
  (= 
    ($A && $A) $A)


  ; Action: load=metta_defn('&self',[A,'||',A],A)
  (= 
    ($A "||" $A) $A)


;;!Extensional set reductions:
  ; Action: load=metta_defn('&self',[[{},A],'|',[{},B]],['{',A,B,'}'])
  (= 
    ( ({} $A) "|" 
      ({} $B)) 
    ({ $A $B }))


  ; Action: load=metta_defn('&self',[['{',A,B,'}'],'|',[{},C]],['{',[A|B],C,'}'])
  (= 
    ( ({ $A $B }) "|" 
      ({} $C)) 
    ({ 
      (Cons  $A $B) $C }))


  ; Action: load=metta_defn('&self',[[{},C],'|',['{',A,B,'}']],['{',C,[A|B],'}'])
  (= 
    ( ({} $C) "|" 
      ({ $A $B })) 
    ({ $C 
      (Cons  $A $B) }))


;;!Intensional set reductions:
  ; Action: load=metta_defn('&self',[[['[]',A]],&,[['[]',B]]],[['[',A,B,']']])
  (= 
    ( ( ([] $A)) & 
      ( ([] $B))) 
    ( ([ $A $B ])))


  ; Action: load=metta_defn('&self',[[['[',A,B,']']],&,[['[]',C]]],[['[',[A|B],C,']']])
  (= 
    ( ( ([ $A $B ])) & 
      ( ([] $C))) 
    ( ([ 
        (Cons  $A $B) $C ])))


  ; Action: load=metta_defn('&self',[[['[]',A]],&,[['[',B,C,']']]],[['[',A,[B|C],']']])
  (= 
    ( ( ([] $A)) & 
      ( ([ $B $C ]))) 
    ( ([ $A 
        (Cons  $B $C) ])))


;;!Reduction for set element copula:
  ; Action: load=metta_defn('&self',[{},[A|B]],['{',A,B,'}'])
  (= 
    ({} 
      (Cons  $A $B)) 
    ({ $A $B }))


  ; Action: load=metta_defn('&self',[['[]',[A|B]]],[['[',A,B,']']])
  (= 
    ( ([] 
        (Cons  $A $B))) 
    ( ([ $A $B ])))

  ; Action: load=metta_defn('&self',[increment,Atom],['change-state!',Atom,[+,1,['get-state',Atom]]])
  (= 
    (increment $Atom) 
    (change-state! $Atom 
      (+ 1 
        (get-state $Atom))))


  ; Action: load=metta_defn('&self',['UpdateReasonerState'],[[increment,'¤tTime'],[increment,'&evidentialBase']])
  (= 
    (UpdateReasonerState) 
    ( (increment ¤tTime) 
      (increment &evidentialBase)))


  ; Action: load=metta_defn('&self',['GetReasonerState'],[['get-state','¤tTime'],[['get-state','&evidentialBase']]])
  (= 
    (GetReasonerState) 
    ( (get-state ¤tTime) 
      ( (get-state &evidentialBase))))


;priority of events
  ; Action: load=metta_defn('&self',['EventPriorityNow',[True,P],True],[*,P,[/,1,[+,1,[-,True,True]]]])
  (= 
    (EventPriorityNow 
      ($True $P) $True) 
    (* $P 
      ("/" 1 
        (+ 1 
          (- $True $True)))))


;retrieve the best candidate (allows to use tuples / collapse results / spaces as a PQ)
!(bind! &tempbest (new-state ()))

 (@ State () $_203704)
 % 'State'([],_203704)

!(bind! &tempbestscore (new-state 0))

 (@ State 0 $_399968)
 % 'State'(0,_399968)

  ; Action: load=metta_defn('&self',['BestCandidate',Tuple,EvaluateCandidateFunction,True],[sequential,[[do,['change-state!','&tempbestscore',0]],[do,['change-state!','&tempbest',[]]],[do,['let*',[[X,[superpose,Tuple]],[Fx,[EvaluateCandidateFunction,X,True]]],[superpose,[['If',[>,Fx,['get-state','&tempbestscore']],[sequential,[['change-state!','&tempbest',X],['change-state!','&tempbestscore',Fx]]]]]]]],['get-state','&tempbest']]])
  (= 
    (BestCandidate $Tuple $EvaluateCandidateFunction $True) 
    (sequential 
      ( (do 
          (change-state! &tempbestscore 0)) 
        (do 
          (change-state! &tempbest ())) 
        (do 
          (let* 
            ( ($X 
                (superpose $Tuple)) 
              ($Fx 
                ($EvaluateCandidateFunction $X $True))) 
            (superpose 
              ( (If 
                  (> $Fx 
                    (get-state &tempbestscore)) 
                  (sequential 
                    ( (change-state! &tempbest $X) 
                      (change-state! &tempbestscore $Fx)))))))) 
        (get-state &tempbest))))


;functions to select highest-priority events in belief and goal PQ
  ; Action: load=metta_defn('&self',['PriorityOf',['Event',Sentence,[OccT,Ev,Prio]],True],['EventPriorityNow',Prio,True])
  (= 
    (PriorityOf 
      (Event $Sentence 
        ($OccT $Ev $Prio)) $True) 
    (EventPriorityNow $Prio $True))

;bound the size of the attentional focus for tasks / events
  ; Action: load=metta_defn('&self',['BoundEvents',Collection,Threshold,Increment,TargetAmount,True],[sequential,[[do,['let*',[[Ev,['get-atoms',Collection]],[['Event',Sentence,[Time,Evidence,EPrio]],Ev]],['If',[<,['EventPriorityNow',EPrio,True],Threshold],['remove-atom',Collection,Ev]]]],[let,CurrentAmount,['CollapseCardinality',['get-atoms',Collection]],['If',[>,CurrentAmount,TargetAmount],['BoundEvents',Collection,[+,Threshold,Increment],Increment,TargetAmount,True]]]]])
  (=

          (let* 
            ( ($Ev

            (If 
              (< 
                (EventPriorityNow $EPrio $True) $Threshold) 
              (remove-atom $Collection $Ev)))) 
        (let $CurrentAmount 
          (CollapseCardinality 
            (get-atoms $Collection)) 
          (If 
            (> $CurrentAmount $TargetAmount) 
            (BoundEvents $Collection 
              (+ $Threshold $Increment) $Increment $TargetAmount $True))))))

  ; Action: load=metta_defn('&self',['RevisionAndChoice',['Event',[Term1,[F1,C1]],[eternal,Ev1,EPrio1]],['Event',[Term2,[F2,C2]],[eternal,Ev2,EPrio2]]],[let,ConclusionStamp,['TupleConcat',Ev1,Ev2],['If',['StampDisjoint',ConclusionStamp],['Event',[Term1,['Truth_Revision',[F1,C1],[F2,C2]]],[eternal,ConclusionStamp,[0,0.0]]],['If',[>,C1,C2],['Event',[Term1,[F1,C1]],[eternal,Ev1,[0,0.0]]],['Event',[Term2,[F2,C2]],[eternal,Ev2,[0,0.0]]]]]])

;making declarative inferences on two events (task from PQ and belief from concept)
  ; Action: load=metta_defn('&self',['Conclude',['Event',S1,[Time1,Ev1,Prio1]],['Event',S2,[Time2,Ev2,Prio2]],CPrio,True],[let,ConclusionStamp,['TupleConcat',Ev1,Ev2],['If',['StampDisjoint',ConclusionStamp],[let,[ConcTerm,ConcTV],[superpose,[['|-',S1,S2],['|-',S2,S1]]],['Event',[ConcTerm,ConcTV],[Time1,ConclusionStamp,[True,['ConclusionPriority',['EventPriorityNow',Prio1,True],['ConceptPriorityNow',CPrio,True],ConcTV]]]]]]])

              ("|-" $S2 $S1)))

            ($Time1 $ConclusionStamp 
              ($True 
                (ConclusionPriority 
                  (EventPriorityNow $Prio1 $True) 
                  (ConceptPriorityNow $CPrio $True) $ConcTV))))))))

;make the belief occurrence time compatible with the task's

;Form a temporal implication between two events
  ; Action: load=metta_defn('&self',['TemporalImplication',Ev1,['Event',[Term2,Truth2],[Time2,Evidence2,EPrio2]]],[let,['Event',[Term1,Truth1],[Time1,Evidence1,EPrio1]],['Projection',Ev1,Time2],['Event',[[Term1,=/>,Term2],['Truth_Induction',Truth1,Truth2]],[Time2,['TupleConcat',Evidence1,Evidence2],[0,0.0]]]])

        ($Term2 $Truth2) 
        ($Time2 $Evidence2 $EPrio2))) 
    (let 
      (Event 
        ($Term1 $Truth1) 
        ($Time1 $Evidence1 $EPrio1)) 
      (Projection $Ev1 $Time2) 
      (Event 
        ( ($Term1 "=/>" $Term2) 
          (Truth_Induction $Truth1 $Truth2)) 
        ($Time2 
          (TupleConcat $Evidence1 $Evidence2) 
          (0 0.0)))))


;Whether an event's term is an operation
  ; Action: load=metta_defn('&self',['IsOp',['Event',[Term,Truth],Metadata]],[case,Term,[[[^,Opname],'True'],[Otherwise,'False']]])
  (= 
    (IsOp 
      (Event 
        ($Term $Truth) $Metadata)) 
    (case $Term 
      ( ( (^ $Opname) True) 
        ($Otherwise False))))


;Find implications in the event FIFO:
;procedural implications
  ; Action: load=metta_defn('&self',['TemporalImplicationInduction',['Cons',Cons,['Cons',Op,['Cons',Prec,Tail]]]],['If',[and,['IsOp',Op],[and,[not,['IsOp',Cons]],[not,['IsOp',Prec]]]],[let,PrecOp,['TemporalSequence',Prec,Op],['TemporalImplication',PrecOp,Cons]]])
  (= 
    (TemporalImplicationInduction 
      (Cons $Cons 
        (Cons $Op 
          (Cons $Prec $Tail)))) 
    (If 
      (and 
        (IsOp $Op) 
        (and 
          (not 
            (IsOp $Cons)) 
          (not 
            (IsOp $Prec)))) 
      (let $PrecOp 
        (TemporalSequence $Prec $Op) 
        (TemporalImplication $PrecOp $Cons))))


;and temporal without operation
  ; Action: load=metta_defn('&self',['TemporalImplicationInduction',['Cons',Cons,['Cons',Prec,Tail]]],['If',[and,[not,['IsOp',Prec]],[not,['IsOp',Cons]]],['TemporalImplication',Prec,Cons]])
  (= 
    (TemporalImplicationInduction 
      (Cons $Cons 
        (Cons $Prec $Tail))) 
    (If 
      (and 
        (not 
          (IsOp $Prec)) 
        (not 
          (IsOp $Cons))) 
      (TemporalImplication $Prec $Cons)))


;Add negative evidence for implications which predicted the input unsuccessfully
  ; Action: load=metta_defn('&self',['NegConfirmation',PrecTerm,ObservedCons,True],[let,['Event',[[PrecTerm,=/>,PredictedCons],ImpTV],ImpMetadata],['EternalQuestion',[PrecTerm,=/>,PredictedCons]],['If',[not,[==,ObservedCons,PredictedCons]],['UpdateConcept',['Event',[[PrecTerm,=/>,PredictedCons],[0.0,0.1]],[True,[],[0,0.0]]],True]]])
  (= 
    (NegConfirmation $PrecTerm $ObservedCons $True) 
    (let 
      (Event 
        ( ($PrecTerm "=/>" $PredictedCons) $ImpTV) $ImpMetadata) 
      (EternalQuestion 
        ($PrecTerm "=/>" $PredictedCons)) 
      (If 
        (not 
          (== $ObservedCons $PredictedCons)) 
        (UpdateConcept 
          (Event 
            ( ($PrecTerm "=/>" $PredictedCons) 
              (0.0 0.1)) 
            ($True () 
              (0 0.0))) $True))))


;Check if the implication's preconditions are met to anticipate the by the implication predicted outcome
  ; Action: load=metta_atom('&self',[=,['Anticipate',['Cons',Pos,[]],True]])
  (= 
    (Anticipate 
      (Cons $Pos ()) $True))


  ; Action: load=metta_defn('&self',['Anticipate',['Cons',Pos,['Cons',Pre,[]]],True],['let*',[[['Event',[PreTerm,PreTV],PreMetadata],Pre],[['Event',[PosTerm,PosTV],PosMetadata],Pos]],['If',[not,['IsOp',Pre]],['NegConfirmation',PreTerm,PosTerm,True]]])
  (= 
    (Anticipate 
      (Cons $Pos 
        (Cons $Pre ())) $True) 
    (let* 
      ( ( (Event 
            ($PreTerm $PreTV) $PreMetadata) $Pre) 
        ( (Event 
            ($PosTerm $PosTV) $PosMetadata) $Pos)) 
      (If 
        (not 
          (IsOp $Pre)) 
        (NegConfirmation $PreTerm $PosTerm $True))))


  ; Action: load=metta_defn('&self',['Anticipate',['Cons',Pos,['Cons',Op,['Cons',Pre,Trail]]],True],['let*',[[['Event',[PreTerm,PreTV],PreMetadata],Pre],[['Event',[OpTerm,OpTV],OpMetadata],Op],[['Event',[PosTerm,PosTV],PosMetadata],Pos],[Sequence,[Pre,&/,'Pos']]],['If',[and,['IsOp',Op],[not,['IsOp',Pre]]],['NegConfirmation',[PreTerm,&/,OpTerm],PosTerm,True]]])
  (= 
    (Anticipate 
      (Cons $Pos 
        (Cons $Op 
          (Cons $Pre $Trail))) $True) 
    (let* 
      ( ( (Event 
            ($PreTerm $PreTV) $PreMetadata) $Pre) 
        ( (Event 
            ($OpTerm $OpTV) $OpMetadata) $Op) 
        ( (Event 
            ($PosTerm $PosTV) $PosMetadata) $Pos) 
        ($Sequence 
          ($Pre "&/" Pos))) 
      (If 
        (and 
          (IsOp $Op) 
          (not 
            (IsOp $Pre))) 
        (NegConfirmation 
          ($PreTerm "&/" $OpTerm) $PosTerm $True))))


;;Input procedure
  ; Action: load=metta_defn('&self',['AddBeliefEvent',Sentence],['let*',[[[True,EvidentialBase],['GetReasonerState']],[InputEvent,['Event',Sentence,[True,EvidentialBase,[True,1.0]]]]],[do,[sequential,[['EventToFIFO',InputEvent],[let,InducedHypothesis,['TemporalImplicationInduction',['get-state','&FIFO']],['UpdateConcept',InducedHypothesis,True]],['ProcessBeliefEvent',InputEvent,True],['Anticipate',['get-state','&FIFO'],True],['BeliefCycle',True]]]]])
  (= 
    (AddBeliefEvent $Sentence) 
    (let* 
      ( ( ($True $EvidentialBase) 
          (GetReasonerState)) 
        ($InputEvent 
          (Event $Sentence 
            ($True $EvidentialBase 
              ($True 1.0))))) 
      (do 
        (sequential 
          ( (EventToFIFO $InputEvent) 
            (let $InducedHypothesis 
              (TemporalImplicationInduction 
                (get-state &FIFO)) 
              (UpdateConcept $InducedHypothesis $True)) 
            (ProcessBeliefEvent $InputEvent $True) 
            (Anticipate 
              (get-state &FIFO) $True) 
            (BeliefCycle $True))))))


;;Procedural inference (decision making with operation execution and subgoaling)
;Derived goal event priority
  ; Action: load=metta_defn('&self',['SubgoalPriority',EPrio,ConcTV],[*,EPrio,['Truth_Expectation',ConcTV]])
  (= 
    (SubgoalPriority $EPrio $ConcTV) 
    (* $EPrio 
      (Truth_Expectation $ConcTV)))


;Expectation of an operation is the truth expectation of its desire value
  ; Action: load=metta_defn('&self',['OpExpectation',['Decision',[Opname,DVOp],Subgoal],True],['Truth_Expectation',DVOp])
  (= 
    (OpExpectation 
      (Decision 
        ($Opname $DVOp) $Subgoal) $True) 
    (Truth_Expectation $DVOp))


;Inject executed operation as an event and return its name
!(assertEqualToResult (sample (FlattenedHybridDist)) (True False Red Green Red Blue False True Green Blue Green Red))

!(assertEqualToResult (sample (FlattenedHybridDist)) (True False Red Green Red Blue False True Green Blue Green Red))

  ; Action: load=metta_defn('&self',['Execute',Opname],[superpose,[['AddBeliefEvent',[Opname,[1.0,0.9]]],Opname]])
  (= 
    (Execute $Opname) 
    (superpose 
      ( (AddBeliefEvent 
          ($Opname 
            (1.0 0.9))) $Opname)))


;Add subgoals to the PQ
  ; Action: load=metta_defn('&self',['DeriveSubgoals',Options],[do,[let,['Decision',Op,Subgoal],[superpose,Options],['add-atom','&goal_events',Subgoal]]])
  (= 
    (DeriveSubgoals $Options) 
    (do 
      (let 
        (Decision $Op $Subgoal) 
        (superpose $Options) 
        (add-atom &goal_events $Subgoal))))


;execute the operation which most likely gets the goal achieved in current contexts, and if contexts are not yet fulfilled, derive them as subgoals
  ; Action: load=metta_defn('&self',['BestDecision',True,['Event',[Term,DV],[GoalTime,GoalEvBase,GoalPrio]],FIFO],[let,Options,[collapse,['let*',[[['Event',[[[Prec,&/,[^,Op]],=/>,Term],ImpTV],[ImpTime,ImpEvBase,ImpPrio]],['EternalQuestion',[[Prec,&/,[^,Op]],=/>,Term]]],[DVPrecOp,['Truth_Deduction',DV,ImpTV]],[['Event',[PrecTerm,PrecTV],PrecMetadata],['Projection',['EventQuestion',Prec],True]],[DVOp,['Truth_Deduction',PrecTV,DVPrecOp]],[DVPrec,['Truth_StructuralDeduction',DVPrecOp]],[SubgoalStamp,['TupleConcat',GoalEvBase,ImpEvBase]]],['If',['StampDisjoint',SubgoalStamp],['Decision',[[^,Op],DVOp],['Event',[Prec,['Truth_StructuralDeduction',DVPrecOp]],[True,SubgoalStamp,[True,['SubgoalPriority',['EventPriorityNow',GoalPrio,True],DVPrec]]]]]]]],[let,['Decision',[Opname,DVOp],Subgoal],['BestCandidate',Options,'OpExpectation',True],['If',[>,['Truth_Expectation',DVOp],0.5],['Execute',Opname],['DeriveSubgoals',Options]]]])
  (= 
    (BestDecision $True 
      (Event 
        ($Term $DV) 
        ($GoalTime $GoalEvBase $GoalPrio)) $FIFO) 
    (let $Options 
      (collapse 
        (let* 
          ( ( (Event 
                ( ( ($Prec "&/" 
                      (^ $Op)) "=/>" $Term) $ImpTV) 
                ($ImpTime $ImpEvBase $ImpPrio)) 
              (EternalQuestion 
                ( ($Prec "&/" 
                    (^ $Op)) "=/>" $Term))) 
            ($DVPrecOp 
              (Truth_Deduction $DV $ImpTV)) 
            ( (Event 
                ($PrecTerm $PrecTV) $PrecMetadata) 
              (Projection 
                (EventQuestion $Prec) $True)) 
            ($DVOp 
              (Truth_Deduction $PrecTV $DVPrecOp)) 
            ($DVPrec 
              (Truth_StructuralDeduction $DVPrecOp)) 
            ($SubgoalStamp 
              (TupleConcat $GoalEvBase $ImpEvBase))) 
          (If 
            (StampDisjoint $SubgoalStamp) 
            (Decision 
              ( (^ $Op) $DVOp) 
              (Event 
                ($Prec 
                  (Truth_StructuralDeduction $DVPrecOp)) 
                ($True $SubgoalStamp 
                  ($True 
                    (SubgoalPriority 
                      (EventPriorityNow $GoalPrio $True) $DVPrec)))))))) 
      (let 
        (Decision 
          ($Opname $DVOp) $Subgoal) 
        (BestCandidate $Options OpExpectation $True) 
        (If 
          (> 
            (Truth_Expectation $DVOp) 0.5) 
          (Execute $Opname) 
          (DeriveSubgoals $Options)))))


;;select the highest priority goal event from the PQ and use it for decision making
  ; Action: load=metta_defn('&self',['GoalCycle',True],[sequential,[[let,Ev,['SelectHighestPriorityEvent','&goal_events',True],[sequential,[[do,['remove-atom','&goal_events',Ev]],['BestDecision',True,Ev,['get-state','&FIFO']]]]],[do,['UpdateReasonerState']],[do,['BoundEvents','&goal_events',0.0,0.1,['GoalEventsMax'],True]]]])
  (= 
    (GoalCycle $True) 
    (sequential 
      ( (let $Ev 
          (SelectHighestPriorityEvent &goal_events $True) 
          (sequential 
            ( (do 
                (remove-atom &goal_events $Ev)) 
              (BestDecision $True $Ev 
                (get-state &FIFO))))) 
        (do 
          (UpdateReasonerState)) 
        (do 
          (BoundEvents &goal_events 0.0 0.1 
            (GoalEventsMax) $True)))))


;;Input procedure
  ; Action: load=metta_defn('&self',['AddGoalEvent',Sentence],['let*',[[[True,EvidentialBase],['GetReasonerState']],[InputEvent,['Event',Sentence,[True,EvidentialBase,[True,1.0]]]]],[sequential,[[do,['add-atom','&goal_events',InputEvent]],['GoalCycle',True]]]])
  (= 
    (AddGoalEvent $Sentence) 
    (let* 
      ( ( ($True $EvidentialBase) 
          (GetReasonerState)) 
        ($InputEvent 
          (Event $Sentence 
            ($True $EvidentialBase 
              ($True 1.0))))) 
      (sequential 
        ( (do 
            (add-atom &goal_events $InputEvent)) 
          (GoalCycle $True)))))
